
# Taskmaster Loop Progress
# Started: 2026-05-21T06:11:50.351Z
# Preset: default
# Max Iterations: 25

---

## Iteration 1 - Task 1: Configure project input map
- Added [input] section to snaketaskmaster/project.godot with 6 actions: move_up/down/left/right (WASD+arrows), start (Enter), restart (R)
- Created test/input_map_test.gd with 7 tests verifying action presence and key bindings
- All tests pass (headless gdUnit4 run)

### Learnings
- Godot project must be imported (`godot --headless --path . --import`) before running gdUnit4 headless, otherwise GdUnitTestCIRunner global class is not registered and the cmd tool fails to parse.

## Iteration 2 - Task 2: Import and configure floor tile sprite
- Copied source/sprites/floor_tile.png to snaketaskmaster/sprites/floor_tile.png
- Ran `godot --headless --import` to generate floor_tile.png.import (defaults already: compress/mode=0 Lossless, mipmaps/generate=false)
- Added project setting `rendering/textures/canvas_textures/default_texture_filter=0` (Nearest) for pixel-art rendering
- Created test/floor_tile_import_test.gd with 3 tests: texture loads, .import params correct, project filter is Nearest
- All tests pass

### Learnings
- In Godot 4, the per-texture "Filter Off (Nearest)" pixel-art setting is NOT in the .import file — it's the project-wide `rendering/textures/canvas_textures/default_texture_filter` setting (0=Nearest, 1=Linear default). Per-sprite override is via CanvasItem.texture_filter.

## Iteration 3 - Task 3: Import and configure wall tile sprite
- Copied source/sprites/wall_tile.png to snaketaskmaster/sprites/wall_tile.png
- Ran `godot --headless --import` — generated wall_tile.png.import with pixel-art defaults (compress/mode=0, mipmaps/generate=false)
- Created test/wall_tile_import_test.gd with 3 tests: texture loads, .import params correct, dimensions match floor_tile
- All tests pass (3/3)

## Iteration 4 - Task 4: Import snake head sprite
- Copied source/sprites/player_head.png to snaketaskmaster/sprites/player_head.png
- Ran `godot --headless --import` — generated player_head.png.import with pixel-art defaults (compress/mode=0, mipmaps/generate=false)
- Created test/player_head_import_test.gd with 3 tests: texture loads, .import params correct, dimensions match floor_tile
- All tests pass (3/3)

## Iteration 5 - Task 5: Import snake body sprite
- Copied source/sprites/player_body.png to snaketaskmaster/sprites/player_body.png
- Ran `godot --headless --import` — generated player_body.png.import with pixel-art defaults (compress/mode=0, mipmaps/generate=false)
- Created test/player_body_import_test.gd with 3 tests: texture loads, .import params correct, dimensions match floor_tile
- All tests pass (3/3)

## Iteration 7 - Task 8: Implement Arena scene with grid-based tilemap
- Created scripts/arena.gd: class Arena extends Node2D with exports grid_width=20, grid_height=15, cell_size=32. Builds TileSet programmatically with floor (source 0) + wall (source 1) atlas sources, populates TileMapLayer with wall perimeter + floor interior in _ready().
- Public API: is_wall(Vector2i) treats perimeter + out-of-bounds as walls; grid_to_world returns cell center; world_to_grid floors world coord into cell index.
- Created scenes/Arena.tscn binding the script to a Node2D root.
- Created test/arena_test.gd with 10 tests covering: default exports, is_wall (corners, edges, interior, out-of-bounds), grid_to_world center placement, world_to_grid floor behavior, round-trip, and tilemap population on _ready (wall vs floor source IDs, tile_size).
- All tests pass (10/10)

## Iteration 10 - Task 11: Implement food spawning logic
- Created scripts/food.gd: class_name Food extends Node2D with const FOOD_TEXTURE preload, position_grid: Vector2i, lazy-created _sprite child, spawn(arena, snake_body) gathers interior cells (1..grid_w-2, 1..grid_h-2) excluding snake_body and uses pick_random(), updates sprite world position via arena.grid_to_world; get_grid_pos() accessor. Empty-valid-cells case returns without mutation.
- Created test/food_test.gd with 6 tests: _ready creates sprite with FOOD_TEXTURE, get_grid_pos returns position_grid, spawn stays in interior bounds (50 iters), never lands on snake body (100 iters), sprite world position matches grid_to_world, deterministic single-cell case (8 of 9 interior cells blocked → always (2,2)). All 6 pass; full suite 55/55.

## Iteration 9 - Task 10: Implement Snake rendering with head and body sprites
- Edited scripts/snake.gd: added HEAD_TEXTURE / BODY_TEXTURE preloads (player_head.png, player_body.png), _sprites: Array[Sprite2D] pool, update_visuals(arena) that grows/shrinks the pool to body.size() and sets each sprite's texture+position+rotation, static _heading_to_angle(h) mapping RIGHT=0, DOWN=PI/2, LEFT=PI, UP=-PI/2. tick() now calls update_visuals(arena) on the non-death path.
- Extended test/snake_test.gd with 7 rendering tests: sprite count matches body, head vs body texture, world positions via arena.grid_to_world, head rotation per cardinal, pool growth/shrink, tick triggers visuals, _heading_to_angle mapping. All 16 tests pass.

## Iteration 8 - Task 9: Implement Snake logic script
- Created scripts/snake.gd: class_name Snake extends Node2D with signals food_eaten + died, exports starting_length=3 and starting_head=(5,7), state body/heading/queued_direction/is_alive.
- reset() rebuilds body horizontally to the left of starting_head (heading right). queue_direction(dir) rejects opposite-heading. tick(arena, food_pos) applies queued_direction, kills on wall or self-collision (per spec), grows on food, pops tail otherwise. Dead snake ignores further ticks.
- Created test/snake_test.gd with 9 tests: starting length, head/heading defaults, queue rejects opposite + accepts perpendicular, tick advances + pops tail, wall collision emits died, self-collision emits died, eating food grows body + emits food_eaten, tick after death is noop.
- All tests pass (9/9)

### Learnings
- After adding a new `class_name X` script that other test files reference, run `godot --headless --path . --import` before the gdUnit4 CLI — otherwise the global class registry isn't refreshed and tests fail to parse with "Cannot infer the type of variable" on any `var x := returns_X()`.

IMPORTANT:
- Complete ONLY ONE task per iteration.
- Keep changes small and focused.
- Do NOT start another task after completing one.
